SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  176 L : SUBJECTS OF THE PAINTINGS Walter Raunig ( Girma Fisseha and Raunig 1985 : 15f. ) has divided the themes of Ethiopian historical painting into nine groups , which he listed according to their frequency : 1 ) religious subjects ; 2 ) the legend of the Queen of Sheba ; 3 ) everyday life ; 4 ) battles ; 5 ) rulers and court , policy and diplomacy ; 6 ) hunting ; 7 ) religious and secular feasts ; 8 ) the fraternization of the animals and various other themes ; and 9 ) court scenes .

SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  200 L : THE STYLE In order to discuss the painting principles of contemporary painting in traditional style I must first characterize the second Gondarene style , which remained the dominant style up to the beginning of the twentieth century , and its transformation , which parallels the principles that Benetta Jules-Rosette has formulated for African art in general in the course of the twentieth century ( 1984 : 37-41 ) .

SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  201 The second Gondarene style was a characteristically sumptuous representative court style , which , according to Chojnacki , was fully developed by around the 1720s ( 2000 : 40 ) , elements of which are preserved in traditional religious paintings and contemporary paintings in traditional style even today .
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  B    0  201 The_AT second_MD_NNT1 Gondarene_NN1@_NP1 style_NN1 was_VBDZ a_AT1 characteristically_RR sumptuous_JJ representative_JJ_NN1 court_NN1 style_NN1 ,_Y which_DDQ ,_Y according_II21 to_II22 Chojnacki_NP1_NN1 ,_Y was_VBDZ fully_RR developed_VVN by_RP%_II around_II the_AT 1720s_MC2 (_Y 2000_MC :_Y 40_MC )_Y ,_Y elements_NN2 of_IO which_DDQ are_VBR preserved_VVN in_II traditional_JJ religious_JJ paintings_NN2 and_CC contemporary_JJ paintings_NN2 in_II traditional_JJ style_NN1 even_RR today_RT ._Y
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  202 Chojnacki ( 1964 : 7 ) formulates the features of this style as follows : as in earlier times , the so-called profile rule was observed , i. e. , morally good individuals were represented in a front view or in a three-quarter position , while the enemies of Christ and the morally bad were represented in profile .

SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  337 In short , traditional painting in Ethiopia has been subject to the following changes : church-trained artists have become rare , except perhaps in Aksum ( Sobania and Silverman , this issue ) , and more self-taught artists are active in rural and urban settings .
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  B    0  337 In_RR21 short_RR22 ,_Y traditional_JJ painting_NN1 in_II Ethiopia_NP1 has_VHZ been_VBN subject_II21 to_II22 the_AT following_JJ changes_NN2 :_Y church-trained_JJ artists_NN2 have_VH0 become_VVN@ rare_JJ ,_Y except_CS perhaps_RR in_II Aksum_NP1_NN1 (_Y Sobania_NP1 and_CC Silverman_NP1_NN1 ,_Y this_DD1 issue_NN1 )_Y ,_Y and_CC more_RGR_DAR self-taught_JJ artists_NN2 are_VBR active_JJ in_II rural_JJ and_CC urban_JJ settings_NN2 ._Y
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  338 Whereas in the past , traditional religious art was acquired by locals , very often in exchange for land rights , painting has developed into a commodity , bought by foreigners , with less direct contact between artist also in line with the wishes of foreign clients , and the style has changed , as is , in general , typical for African art when foreigners enter in large numbers .
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  B    0  338 Whereas_CS in_II the_AT past_NN1 ,_Y traditional_JJ religious_JJ art_NN1 was_VBDZ acquired_VVN by_II locals_NN2 ,_Y very_RG often_RR in_II exchange_NN1 for_IF land_NN1 rights_NN2 ,_Y painting_NN1 has_VHZ developed_VVN into_II a_AT1 commodity_NN1 ,_Y bought_VVN by_II foreigners_NN2 ,_Y with_IW less_RGR_DAR direct_JJ contact_NN1 between_II artist_NN1 also_RR in_II31 line_II32 with_II33 the_AT wishes_NN2 of_IO foreign_JJ clients_NN2 ,_Y and_CC the_AT style_NN1 has_VHZ changed_VVN ,_Y as_CSA is_VBZ ,_Y in_RR21 general_RR22 ,_Y typical_JJ for_IF African_JJ art_NN1 when_RRQ_CS foreigners_NN2 enter_VV0 in_II_RP@ large_JJ numbers_NN2 ._Y
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_00_FILE##4070609 COCA  A    0  339 The result of all these changes is that contemporary painting in traditional style probably is in the process of being superseded by tourist art manufactured by institutions like the Ethiopian Handicraft Center and ETTE as well as by the products of painters trained at the SFAD .
